<table>

<tr>

</th>
<td>3 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Publication
</th>
<td>1795 in <i><a href="/wiki/Piano_Trios,_Op.82_(Haydn,_Joseph)" title="Piano Trios, Op.82 (Haydn, Joseph)">Piano Trios, Op.82</a></i> (No.2)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Trios&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Trios</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_violin%2C_cello%2C_piano&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For violin, cello, piano</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_violin&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the violin</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="17 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_cello&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the cello</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_piano&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the piano</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Known as the "Gypsy" or the 3rd movement as the "Gypsy Rondo".
